GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A*exp(-c3*_s*t) + c4*_w*cos(log(A + c5))
Candidate formulas: 50

I need to find a candidate that can match the GT:
`-0.5475*A² - 0.5475*A*exp(-0.0371*t) + 0.7049*cos(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three terms:
1. A² term (with coefficient -0.5475)
2. A*exp(αt) term (with α ≈ -0.0371)
3. cos(log(A+1)) term (with coefficient ≈ 0.7049)

Let me look for candidates that can produce a `cos(log(A+c))` term, since that's the most distinctive part.

**Candidate 13**: `A^c0 * c1 + c2*t*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8+1) + c9)`

This has:
- `A^c0 * c1`: set c0=2, giving c1*A²
- `c2*t*exp(c3*t)`: no pure A*exp(αt) term available
- `c4*exp(c5*t)`: exponential in t only
- `c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8+1) + c9)`: This is key! Using sin with a phase shift: sin(x + π/2) = cos(x)

So setting c9 = π/2, c7 = 1, c8 = 1: `c6*sin(log(A+1) + π/2) = c6*cos(log(A+1))` ✓

But the GT has `A*exp(-0.0371*t)`, and candidate 13 only has `c2*t*exp(c3*t)` and `c4*exp(c5*t)` — neither can produce `A*exp(αt)`. So candidate 13 doesn't work.

**Candidate 34**: `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2/(c3+t) + c4*sin(A*c5 + c6*t + c7)`

This has `sin(A*c5 + c6*t + c7)` which is sin of a linear function of A, not sin(log(A+1)). Can't match.

**Candidate 29**: `c0 + c1*exp(c2*t) + c3/(A+c4) + c5*log(A*c6+1) + c7*exp(c8*t)*log(A*c9+1)`

This has log terms, not cos(log) terms. Can't match.

**Candidate 48**: `A^c0 * c1 + c2*t*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8) + 1)`

The last term: `c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8) + 1)`. This is not cos(log(...)). Can't match.

Let me reconsider. The cos(log(A+1)) term is very specific. Let me check if any candidate can replicate it through some algebraic identity.

Looking through all candidates more carefully, none seem to have trigonometric functions except candidates 13 and 34.

**Candidate 13 revisited**: The sin term can become cos(log(A+1)), and A^c0*c1 can give A². But we need A*exp(αt). We have c2*t*exp(c3*t) and c4*exp(c5*t). Setting c2=0 eliminates the t*exp term. Then c4*exp(c5*t) is only a function of t, not A*exp(αt). So this fails.

No candidate has both:
- A cos(log(A+c)) or equivalent
- A*exp(αt) (A times exponential in t)

None of the candidates can simultaneously produce A², A*exp(αt), and cos(log(A+1)).

Only candidates 13 and 34 have trig functions. Candidate 34 has sin of a linear function, not of log. Candidate 13 has sin(log(...)) but can't produce both A² and A*exp(αt).

The GT has three terms:
1. A quadratic term in A: `-0.5475*A²`
2. An exponential decay term: `-0.5475*A*exp(-0.0371*t)`
3. A cosine of logarithm term: `0.7049*cos(log(A+1))`

The key challenge is that `cos(log(A+1))` is a very specific basis function. Let me check which candidates could potentially contain or reproduce this function.

**Key observation:** `cos(log(A+1))` cannot be represented by polynomials in A, exponentials of A, simple rational functions of A, or `log(A+1)` alone. It requires either an explicit `cos(log(...))` term, or a `sin`/`cos` combined with `log`, or some equivalent.

Let me scan candidates for those containing trigonometric or cosine-of-log type terms:

- **Candidate 13:** Has `sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)` - this could match `cos(log(A+1))` via phase shift!
- **Candidate 34:** Has `sin(A*c5 + c6*t + c7)` - sin of linear function, not log
- **Candidate 48:** Has `log(c7*exp(A*c8) + 1)` - this is a softplus, not trig

Let me analyze **Candidate 13** in detail:
`A^c0 * c1 + c2*t*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*sin(c7*log(A*c8 + 1) + c9)`

- Set c0=2, c1=-0.5475 → `-0.5475*A²` ✓
- `sin(c7*log(c8*A + 1) + c9)`: Set c7=1, c8=1, c9=π/2 → `sin(log(A+1) + π/2) = cos(log(A+1))`, with c6=0.7049 ✓
- For the A*exp term: GT has `-0.5475*A*exp(-0.0371*t)`. But Candidate 13 has `c2*t*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*t)`, neither of which contains A multiplied by exp(t). The GT requires a term `A*exp(αt)` which is absent here.

So Candidate 13 cannot match because it lacks the `A*exp(t)` coupling.

Now let me check all other candidates systematically. Almost all candidates lack `cos(log(...))` or any equivalent trigonometric-logarithmic composition. The only candidates with trig functions are 13 and 34, and 34 uses `sin(A*c5 + c6*t + c7)` which is sin of a linear function, not sin/cos of log.

None of the remaining candidates have any mechanism to produce `cos(log(A+1))`. This function cannot be approximated by:
- Polynomials in A
- Rational functions of A
- `exp(A)` or `exp(A²)`
- `log(A+1)` (without cosine wrapper)
- Products of the above

Since `cos(log(A+1))` is linearly independent from all polynomial, rational, exponential, and logarithmic basis functions, no candidate without an explicit trigonometric composition with logarithm can match.

**Candidate 13** is the closest but lacks the `A*exp(αt)` term, so it fails.

Let me verify all candidates one final time for any I might have missed with trig(log(...)) structure: Only Candidate 13 has this. No match.
